<Resp>None<//Resp>< Text>
I‚Äôve been on the hunt recently for a good San Diego Poke bowl. After a recent disappointment where I tossed half my bowl, I wanted to redeem the search!

This place is simple. They have a set menu of poke bowl options, so I chose traditional. The poke was fresh (tho diced a bit large for my taste). The avocado was good (but had some brown spots).  It also came with seaweed salad (yummy). But...no sauce at all! Is this usual? My friend and I got one small container of soy sauce for both of us and three siracha packets to share.

It was a good, fresh poke bowl‚Äî but a little too simple. I prefer to have a few more toppings and the fish a bit more bite sized.< /Text>

< review>
This is for a visit this past summer, but when something sticks with you then you know it is good. My day getting into Pacific Beach was less than stellar and involved a lack of coffee and breakfast. So I started off behind schedule and grumpy. Decided on an early lunch as I had graduated to hangry and had my life flash before my eyes when another driver drove the wrong way in my lane to get to where they wanted to be a little faster.  So I pull into this little place hangry and shook up and I'm beyond hope for ordering. I explain what happened and just ask them to make something they'd like, not too spicy. WOW! I may have to try that more often. It was perfect. So good in fact that when I was back in that area the following week it was my place to go for lunch that day too. I didn't know what I'd eaten the time before, but I picked some things I wanted to eat and described some of what I had the week before and had another winning dish. Will definitely be visiting the next time I'm headed to PB.</review>

4< /rating>
< text>
Very fresh ingredients and prepared with care. Clean interior and you can see what goes on in the kitchen, which is always a plus.
Portion size is smaller than other poke places (and there are tons of them nowadays). The Signature bowls are smaller servings than the Build your own and are more expensive, therefore not a good deal. I ordered the "Rub my Belly" (with torched salmon belly) for $15 and it had 3 ingredients - salmon, rice and avocado. Friends built their own and had much more food for less money.
Anyway, place is good, fresh and clean so I can recommend it with clear conscience.< /text>

< Review>
This is a small little bakery with Portuguese goods. It's been around since the mid 80s and I've barely discovered it just recently. Their Past√©is de Natas which are Portuguese custard tarts are so delicious!! It's almost as good as the ones from Past√©is de Bel√©m in Lisbon, Portugal. The crust is nice and soft, a little flaky on the outside with creamy custard inside. If you like, you can also warm it up at home and add powdered sugar and cinnamon on top just like they do in Portugal. But it is really good just the way it is. I'm so glad I found this bakery, it's probably the best Past√©is de Natas I've had so far in the Bay Area. I'm also going to try other places to compare. I'll most definitely come back here for their Past√©is de Natas again. They tend to run out so I suggest calling in ahead of time to let them know you're coming in for Past√©is de Nata and they will keep some for you.

I've tried their almond and cream puff pastry and it was okay.< /Review>

My life partner, Jerry has been a customer of picknpull since they opened ( usually Richmond yard and occasionally Oakland).  We know their policies and haven't ever had a problem.
Jerry is a retired veteran, and has been a self- employed mechanic for a very long time.
Recently we moved to Vallejo so have been going to the Fairfield yard more. We thought we would check out the new American canyon yard.

So he ended up pulling a motor from an Impala for a client of his from this yard for $310 on 10/27. Took it home and installed it. Took the core in on 10/31 (the cashier neglected to return the original receipt of the purchase - although he didn't realize this until days later).
The motor ended up having a cracked head, so he took it back to that yard and was expecting to get the credit due him so he could find another motor to replace it but instead got told that he would get a call, which we never recieved ( this was when he realized the receipt was not in his possession anymore).
RICHMOND ALWAYS STAPLED THE ORIGINAL PURCHASE RECEIPT TO THE CORE RECEIPT -KUDOS TO RICHMOND!.
So, on the next Monday, we took the motor back (again) and asked for Sonny, the manager. And because we didn't have the original receipt ( but we had the core receipt which has a reference to the original receipt's number on it) - he said he couldn't (wouldn't, actually)do anything for Jerry!!
We put a complaint in;  another one to Schnitzer; contacted the Ethics point company; contacted 7 on your side; no response from anyone!!
THIS HELLA IRKS US!! ALL HE WANTS IS THE $280 CREDIT THAT IS RIGHTFULLY HIS!! THE CASHIER IS THE ONE AT FAULT HERE! THERE IS NO WAY TO PROVE THAT, THOUGH. SO THE CUSTOMER LOSES! SO MUCH FOR THE STATEMENTS MADE UNDER THE 'INTEGRITY' PART OF THE COMPANY POLICIES! THIS IS ONLY
REGARDING THE PICKNPULL YARD AT AMERCAN CANYON! THEY SUCK!< /text>

* Wanton soup - I thought it is wantin noddle soup but it was just wanton soup. There were avfew wantons, a few vegies and few meat. The amount was too small. My boyfriend ordered it and ate all for few minutes. If u want a meal, it will be better to order wanton noddle soup.

Taste was soso. Nothing special. The quality of wanton and soup was not really good.

<Rating>2< /Rating>< review>
We chose Old Siam due to it's amazing proximity to our hotel and the amount of vegetarian options available compared to other Thai restaurants nearby. However, we feel it was a bad choice. I knew going in not to expect very high class service, but we weren't even offered water. We had to ask for it outright once the food came. The food itself was not very good. The fried rice was lacking salt, or some similar seasoning, badly. It was extremely bland. The pad Thai was slightly better but nothing to write home about. Also our table of 2 had an automatic 18% gratituity added, which wasn't advertised at all, and we found extremely strange. The only good thing I can say it that it was quick.< /review>

Mg 0<//username>
< Review>
Really kind, attentive, service-focussed employees at this tasty old-school Thai restaurant.Went here on a recent Friday night for dinner with a friend, sister and infant and were promptly seated and attended to. Two of us got the large bowls of pho-like "fresh beef" (we guessed, seemingly correctly, that "fresh" was code word for "raw") soup, in which they kindly replaced noodles with various vegetables, which also had a surprising, and happy, quantity of tender beef tendon in it. The broth was flavoursome, complex, with notable flavours of star anise and Szechuan pepper. It was a bit on the salty side, but delicious.
We also got the pad see ew with chicken, and liked its layered tastes and the chewiness of the wide rice noodles. The total for the 3 of us came to about $35, including a beer.
Really appreciated the welcoming atmosphere and the fact that the the music was kept at a low volume!<//Review>
